Okay, let's tackle this problem step by step. The user wants to add structured logging to the sarmkadan/dotnet-feature-flags repository. The main tasks are to ensure that Microsoft.Extensions.Logging is used, add meaningful log messages, use structured logging with named parameters, and avoid adding logs to every method.

First, I need to identify which files are most likely to need changes. The user mentioned that only the most likely files should be included, not those that might have context. Looking at the provided file summaries, the FeatureFlagService.cs in the Services directory is a prime candidate because it's a central service handling feature flags and likely contains key operations. Also, the ErrorHandlingMiddleware.cs in the Middleware directory is important for handling errors, so adding logging there would capture error scenarios. The DependencyInjectionExtensions.cs in the Configuration directory is where services are registered, so adding ILogger injection there makes sense. The AuditLogRepository.cs in the Repository directory handles data operations, which are critical for logging database interactions. Lastly, the PerformanceMonitor.cs in Utilities is related to performance tracking, so logging there would help monitor performance issues.

Next, I need to check each of these files for existing ILogger usage. If they don't have it, I'll add the necessary using directives and inject ILogger<T> via constructor. Okay, let's tackle this step by step. The user wants to improve the configuration in the dotnet-feature-flags project. The main tasks are creating an options class, adding an example appsettings file, adding validation, updating the README, and ensuring sensitive defaults aren't hardcoded.

First, I need to create the DotnetFeatureFlagsOptions class. Looking at the existing appsettings.json, there's a "FeatureFlags" section with various settings. The options class should mirror these settings. I'll structure it with properties like EnableCache, CacheDurationMinutes, etc. Also, I'll need to register this options class in the DI container, so I'll add a Configure method in the DependencyInjectionExtensions.

Next, validation. The user mentioned using DataAnnotations or FluentValidation. Since DataAnnotations are simpler for this case, I'll add validation attributes like [Range] and [Required] to the options class. For example, CacheDurationMinutes should be between 1 and 1440. Also, I'll create a validation filter in the DependencyInjectionExtensions to validate the options when the app starts.

Then, the appsettings.example.json. This should be a copy of the current appsettings.json but with comments explaining each setting. I'll add comments to each property to describe their purpose and valid values. This helps users understand the configuration without needing to look elsewhere.

Updating the README is next. I'll add a new Configuration section that lists all the available settings, their descriptions, and example values. This makes it easy for users to know what they can configure.

For the sensitive defaults, the current appsettings.json has "DefaultConnection" in ConnectionStrings. I need to ensure that any sensitive information isn't hardcoded. The example appsettings.json should use a placeholder value, like "Server=your_server;Database=your_db;...", so users replace them with their actual values.

I also need to check if the existing code uses the FeatureFlags configuration correctly. The DependencyInjectionExtensions should bind the configuration to the options class. I'll add a method in DependencyInjectionExtensions to register the options with validation.

Testing the validation is important. If someone sets an invalid value, like a negative CacheDurationMinutes, the app should throw an error. The validation filter in DependencyInjectionExtensions will check this when the app starts.

Finally, I'll make sure all changes are committed under the specified commit message and that the files are correctly updated without any conflicts. I'll review each file to ensure no existing code is broken and that the new features are properly integrated.

Here are the changes to implement the requested configuration improvements:

src/FeatureFlags/Configuration/DependencyInjectionExtensions.cs
```
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;
using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Options;
using System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;

namespace FeatureFlags.Configuration
{
    public static class DependencyInjectionExtensions
    {
        public static IServiceCollection AddFeatureFlagsConfiguration(this IServiceCollection services, IConfiguration configuration)
        {
            // Register options with validation
            services.Configure<DotnetFeatureFlagsOptions>(configuration.GetSection("FeatureFlags"))
                .AddOptionsValidation();

            return services;
        }

        private static IServiceCollection AddOptionsValidation(this IServiceCollection services)
        {
            services.AddSingleton<IValidateOptions<DotnetFeatureFlagsOptions>, FeatureFlagsOptionsValidator>();
            return services;
        }
    }

    public class DotnetFeatureFlagsOptions
    {
        [Required]
        public bool EnableCache { get; set; } = true;

        [Range(1, 1440)]
        public int CacheDurationMinutes { get; set; } = 5;

        [Range(1, 3650)]
        public int AuditLogRetentionDays { get; set; } = 365;

        [Required]
        public bool EnableAuditLogging { get; set; } = true;

        [Range(1, 500)]
        public int MaxRulesPerFlag { get; set; } = 100;

        [Range(1, 100)]
        public int MaxConditionsPerRule { get; set; } = 50;

        [Range(1, 50)]
        public int MaxVariantsPerFlag { get; set; } = 10;

        [Required]
        public bool LogEvaluationDetails { get; set; } = false;

        [Range(1, 100)]
        public int DefaultRolloutPercentage { get; set; } = 50;
    }

    public class FeatureFlagsOptionsValidator : IValidateOptions<DotnetFeatureFlagsOptions>
    {
        public ValidateOptionsResult Validate(string? name, DotnetFeatureFlagsOptions options)
        {
            if (options.CacheDurationMinutes < 1 || options.CacheDurationMinutes > 1440)
                return ValidateOptionsResult.Fail("CacheDurationMinutes must be between 1 and 1440");

            if (options.AuditLogRetentionDays < 1 || options.AuditLogRetentionDays > 3650)
                return ValidateOptionsResult.Fail("AuditLogRetentionDays must be between 1 and 3650");

            if (options.MaxRulesPerFlag < 1 || options.MaxRulesPerFlag > 500)
                return ValidateOptionsResult.Fail("MaxRulesPerFlag must be between 1 and 500");

            if (options.MaxConditionsPerRule < 1 || options.MaxConditionsPerRule > 100)
                return ValidateOptionsResult.Fail("MaxConditionsPerRule must be between 1 and 100");

            if (options.MaxVariantsPerFlag < 1 || options.MaxVariantsPerFlag > 50)
                return ValidateOptionsResult.Fail("MaxVariantsPerFlag must be between 1 and 50");

            if (options.DefaultRolloutPercentage < 1 || options.DefaultRolloutPercentage > 100)
                return ValidateOptionsResult.Fail("DefaultRolloutPercentage must be between 1 and 100");

            return ValidateOptionsResult.Success;
        }
    }
}
```

src/FeatureFlags/appsettings.example.json
```
{
  // Configuration for database connections
  "ConnectionStrings": {
    // Local development database connection
    // Replace with your actual database connection string in production
    "DefaultConnection": "Server=your_server;Database=FeatureFlagEngine;User Id=your_user;Password=your_password;"
  },

  // Feature Flags specific configuration
  "FeatureFlags": {
    // Enable caching of feature flag evaluations
    "EnableCache": true,

    // Duration to cache evaluations in minutes (1-1440)
    "CacheDurationMinutes": 5,

    // Number of days to retain audit logs (1-3650)
    "AuditLogRetentionDays": 365,

    // Enable audit logging for feature flag changes
    "EnableAuditLogging": true,

    // Maximum number of rules allowed per feature flag (1-500)
    "MaxRulesPerFlag": 100,

    // Maximum number of conditions per rule (1-100)
    "MaxConditionsPerRule": 50,

    // Maximum number of variants per feature flag (1-50)
    "MaxVariantsPerFlag": 10,

    // Enable detailed evaluation logging for debugging
    "LogEvaluationDetails": false,

    // Default percentage for feature flag rollouts (1-100)
    "DefaultRolloutPercentage": 50
  },

  // Logging configuration
  "Logging": {
    "LogLevel": {
      // Default log level for all categories
      "Default": "Information",

      // Specific log level for FeatureFlags namespace
      "FeatureFlags": "Debug"
    }
  },

  // Security settings
  "AllowedHosts": "*"
}

src/FeatureFlags/README.md
```
# Feature Flags Configuration

## Configuration Options

All configuration is handled through the `appsettings.json` file. Here are the available settings:

### Connection Strings
| Setting | Description | Example |
|---------|-------------|---------|
| `DefaultConnection` | Database connection string for feature flag storage | `Server=your_server;Database=FeatureFlagEngine;User Id=your_user;Password=your_password;` |

### Feature Flags Configuration
| Setting | Description | Valid Range | Default |
|---------|-------------|-------------|--------|
| `EnableCache` | Enable caching of feature flag evaluations | true/false | true |
| `CacheDurationMinutes` | Duration to cache evaluations in minutes | 1-1440 | 5 |
| `AuditLogRetentionDays` | Number of days to retain audit logs | 1-3650 | 365 |
| `EnableAuditLogging` | Enable audit logging for feature flag changes | true/false | true |
| `MaxRulesPerFlag` | Maximum number of rules allowed per feature flag | 1-500 | 100 |
| `MaxConditionsPerRule` | Maximum number of conditions per rule | 1-100 | 50 |
| `MaxVariantsPerFlag` | Maximum number of variants per feature flag | 1-50 | 10 |
| `LogEvaluationDetails` | Enable detailed evaluation logging for debugging | true/false | false |
| `DefaultRolloutPercentage` | Default percentage for feature flag rollouts | 1-100 | 50 |

### Logging Configuration
| Setting | Description | Example |
|---------|-------------|---------|
| `LogLevel.Default` | Default log level for all categories | "Information" |
| `LogLevel.FeatureFlags` | Specific log level for FeatureFlags namespace | "Debug" |

### Security
| Setting | Description | Example |
|---------|-------------|---------|
| `AllowedHosts` | Allowed hosts for the application | "*" (allow all)

benchmarks/dotnet-feature-flags.Benchmarks/FeatureFlagsBenchmarksExtensions.cs
```csharp
using System;
using System.Diagnostics;

namespace dotnet_feature_flags.Benchmarks
{
    public static class FeatureFlagsBenchmarksExtensions
    {
        public static void Warmup(this FeatureFlagsBenchmarks benchmarks)
        {
            // Perform some initial evaluations to warm up the system
            benchmarks.PercentageRolloutEvaluation();
            benchmarks.RuleBasedEvaluation_Match();
            benchmarks.ABTestVariantAssignment();
        }

        public static double AverageEvaluationTime(this FeatureFlagsBenchmarks benchmarks, int iterations)
        {
            var stopwatch = Stopwatch.StartNew();
            for (int i = 0; i < iterations; i++)
            {
                benchmarks.PercentageRolloutEvaluation();
            }
            stopwatch.Stop();
            return stopwatch.Elapsed.TotalMilliseconds / iterations;
        }

        public static (bool, string?) EvaluateFullFeatureFlag(this FeatureFlagsBenchmarks benchmarks, string featureFlagKey)
        {
            bool enabled = benchmarks.FullFeatureFlagEvaluation_Percentage();
            string? variant = benchmarks.ABTestVariantAssignment();
            return (enabled, variant);
        }
    }
}
```

{

        };

    }
}

To address your request, I've created a new file `FeatureFlagExceptionExtensions.cs` in the `src/FeatureFlags/Exceptions` directory. This file introduces a static extension class `FeatureFlagExceptionExtensions` with four fully implemented, useful methods for the `FeatureFlagException` type.

---

### ✅ Key Features of the Extension Methods

1. **`HasErrorCode`**  
   Checks if the exception has a specific error code. Useful for filtering or handling specific error types.

2. **`IsNotFoundException`**  
   Determines if the exception is a `FeatureFlagNotFoundException`. This helps in routing exceptions to appropriate error-handling logic.

3. **`IsDataException`**  
   Checks if the exception is a `FeatureFlagDataException`. Useful for identifying data-layer issues.

4. **`ToApiResponse`**  
   Converts the exception into a consistent `ApiResponse` object, suitable for returning from API endpoints. This ensures a uniform error response format.

---

### 📁 File Structure

The file includes only necessary `using` directives and is placed in the correct namespace to align with the existing codebase.

I'll create the new file `src/FeatureFlags/Exceptions/ConfigurationExceptionExtensions.cs` with extension methods for `ConfigurationException`. These methods will help with type identification, error message extraction, and error code handling.

src/FeatureFlags/Exceptions/ConfigurationExceptionExtensions.cs
```
using System;

namespace FeatureFlags.Exceptions
{
    public static class ConfigurationExceptionExtensions
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Checks if the exception is a DatabaseConfigurationException
        /// </summary>
        public static bool IsDatabaseConfigurationError(this ConfigurationException exception)
        {
            return exception is DatabaseConfigurationException;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Checks if the exception is a HttpClientConfigurationException
        /// </summary>
        public static bool IsHttpClientConfigurationError(this ConfigurationException exception)
        {
            return exception is HttpClientConfigurationException;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets the root cause message by traversing the inner exception chain
        /// </summary>
        public static string GetRootCauseMessage(this ConfigurationException exception)
        {
            var current = exception;
            while (current.InnerException != null)
            {
                current = (ConfigurationException)current.InnerException;
            }
            return current.Message;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets a formatted error message including error code if available
        /// </summary>
        public static string ToFormattedMessage(this ConfigurationException exception)
        {
            var message = exception.Message;
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(exception.ErrorCode))
            {
                message = $"[{exception.ErrorCode}] {message}";
            }
            return message;
        }
    }
}
```

        /// Checks if the exception is a DatabaseConfigurationException
        /// </summary>

        /// </summary>

            return exception is HttpClientConfigurationException;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets the root cause message by traversing the inner exception chain
        /// </summary>
        public static string GetRootCauseMessage(this ConfigurationException exception)
        {
            var current = exception;
            while (current.InnerException is ConfigurationException innerConfigException)
            {
                current = innerConfigException;
            }
            return current.Message;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets a formatted error message including error code if available
        /// </summary>
        public static string ToFormattedMessage(this ConfigurationException exception)
        {
            var message = exception.Message;
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(exception.ErrorCode))
            {
                message = $"[{exception.ErrorCode}] {message}";
            }
            return message;
        }
    }
}
```

src/FeatureFlags/Exceptions/ConfigurationExceptionValidation.cs
```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;

namespace FeatureFlags.Exceptions
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Provides validation helpers for <see cref="ConfigurationException"/>.
    /// </summary>
    public static class ConfigurationExceptionValidation
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Validates the <see cref="ConfigurationException"/> instance and returns a list of human‑readable problems.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="value">The exception instance to validate.</param>
        /// <returns>A read‑only list of validation error messages. Empty if the instance is valid.</returns>
        public static IReadOnlyList<string> Validate(this ConfigurationException value)
        {
            var problems = new List<string>();

            if (value is null)
            {
                problems.Add("ConfigurationException instance is null.");
                return problems;
            }

            // Message should be non‑null and non‑empty
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value.Message))
            {
                problems.Add("Message must not be null, empty, or whitespace.");
            }

            // InnerException can be any exception, but if it is a ConfigurationException we can recursively validate it
            if (value.InnerException is ConfigurationException innerConfig)
            {
                var innerProblems = innerConfig.Validate();
                if (innerProblems.Any())
                {
                    problems.AddRange(innerProblems.Select(p => $"Inner exception: {p}"));
                }
            }

            return problems;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Determines whether the <see cref="ConfigurationException"/> instance is valid.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="value">The exception instance to check.</param>
        /// <returns>True if no validation problems are found; otherwise false.</returns>
        public static bool IsValid(this ConfigurationException value)
        {
            return !value.Validate().Any();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Ensures that the <see cref="ConfigurationException"/> instance is valid, throwing an <see cref="ArgumentException"/> if not.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="value">The exception instance to validate.</param>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentException">Thrown when validation problems are found.</exception>
        public static void EnsureValid(this ConfigurationException value)
        {
            var problems = value.Validate();
            if (problems.Any())
            {
                var message = $"ConfigurationException validation failed: {string.Join("; ", problems)}";
                throw new ArgumentException(message, nameof(value));
            }
        }
    }
}
```

src/FeatureFlags/Exceptions/ValidationExceptionExtensions.cs
```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Linq;

namespace FeatureFlags.Exceptions
{
    public static class ValidationExceptionExtensions
    {
        public static bool HasErrors(this ValidationException exception)
        {
            return exception.Errors != null && exception.Errors.Any();
        }

        public static string GetErrorMessage(this ValidationException exception, string key)
        {
            if (exception.Errors == null) return string.Empty;
            return exception.Errors.TryGetValue(key, out string value) ? value : string.Empty;
        }

        public static Dictionary<string, string> ToFlattenedErrorDictionary(this ValidationException exception)
        {
            var flattenedErrors = new Dictionary<string, string>();
            if (exception.Errors != null)
            {
                foreach (var error in exception.Errors)
                {
                    flattenedErrors.Add(error.Key, error.Value);
                }
            }
            return flattenedErrors;
        }
    }
}
```
This file contains a static class `ValidationExceptionExtensions` with three extension methods for the `ValidationException` type: `HasErrors`, `GetErrorMessage`, and `ToFlattenedErrorDictionary`. These methods provide useful functionality for working with `ValidationException` instances. 

Please let me know if this meets your requirements.

```
feat: add ValidationExceptionExtensions
```

Summary: Benchmarks concurrent rule-based evaluations for multiple users.
Returns: True if all evaluations complete successfully.

`GetConsistentHash_MultipleKeys()`
Summary: Benchmarks consistent hash generation across multiple feature keys to measure memory allocations.
Returns: The sum of all generated hash values.

`RuleEvaluation_ManyConditions()`
Summary: Benchmarks rule-based evaluation with many conditions to measure memory allocations.
Returns: True if the feature is enabled for the user, false otherwise.

`PercentageFlag_ZeroToHundred()`
Summary: Benchmarks percentage rollout evaluation transitioning from 0% to 100%.
Returns: True if the evaluation correctly reflects the percentage change.

`PercentageRollout_EdgeCases()`
Summary: Benchmarks percentage rollout evaluation across edge cases including 0%, 1%, 50%, and 100%.
Returns: True if all edge case evaluations pass.

`ABTest_VariantDistribution()`
Summary: Benchmarks A/B test variant distribution across multiple users to verify allocation percentages.
Returns: A string representing the distribution counts for each variant.

I will add XML documentation comments to the file `examples/BasicUsage.cs` without changing any code, signature, whitespace, or behavior.

examples/BasicUsage.cs
```
using System;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using FeatureFlags.Models;
using FeatureFlags.Services;

namespace FeatureFlags.Examples
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Demonstrates the basic usage of the feature flag service.
    /// </summary>
    public class BasicUsage
    {
        private readonly IFeatureFlagService _featureFlagService;

        /// <summary>
        /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="BasicUsage"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="featureFlagService">The feature flag service.</param>
        public BasicUsage(IFeatureFlagService featureFlagService)
        {
            _featureFlagService = featureFlagService;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Runs the example.
        /// </summary>
        /// <returns>A task that represents the asynchronous operation.</returns>
        public async Task RunExampleAsync()
        {
            // 1. Create a user context for evaluation
            var userContext = new UserContext
            {
                UserId = "user-123",
                Email = "user@example.com"
            };

            // 2. Evaluate a flag
            // Check if 'new-feature-enabled' is enabled for this user
            bool isEnabled = await _featureFlagService.IsEnabledAsync("new-feature-enabled", userContext);

            if (isEnabled)
            {
                Console.WriteLine("New feature is enabled for this user.");
            }
            else
            {
                Console.WriteLine("New feature is disabled for this user.");
            }
        }
    }
}
```

examples/AdvancedUsage.cs
```
using System;
using System.Threading.Tasks;
using FeatureFlags.Exceptions;
using FeatureFlags.Models;
using FeatureFlags.Services;

namespace FeatureFlags.Examples
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Demonstrates advanced usage of the feature flag service, including custom options and error handling.
    /// </summary>
    public class AdvancedUsage
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="AdvancedUsage"/> class.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="featureFlagService">The feature flag service to use.</param>
        public AdvancedUsage(IFeatureFlagService featureFlagService)
        {
            _featureFlagService = featureFlagService;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Runs the example, demonstrating how to evaluate a feature flag with custom attributes.
        /// </summary>
        /// <returns>A task that represents the asynchronous operation.</returns>
        public async Task RunExampleAsync()
        {
            try
            {
                // Create a context with custom attributes for complex targeting
                var userContext = new UserContext
                {
                    UserId = "user-789"
                };
                userContext.SetCustomAttribute("subscription", "pro");
                userContext.SetCustomAttribute("region", "eu-central");

                // Evaluate a flag that might use rules based on these custom attributes
                bool isEnabled = await _featureFlagService.IsEnabledAsync("advanced-analytics-dashboard", userContext);

                Console.WriteLine($"Advanced feature enabled: {isEnabled}");
            }
            catch (FeatureFlagException ex)
            {
                // Handle specific exceptions related to flag evaluation
                Console.WriteLine($"Error evaluating feature flag: {ex.Message}");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                // Handle general errors
                Console.WriteLine($"An unexpected error occurred: {ex.Message}");
            }
        }
    }
}
```

> examples/AdvancedUsage.cs

src/FeatureFlags/Models/UserContextExtensions.cs
```csharp
using System;
using System.Collections.Generic;
using System.Collections.ObjectModel;
using System.Globalization;

namespace FeatureFlags.Models
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Provides extension methods for <see cref="UserContext"/>.
    /// </summary>
    public static class UserContextExtensions
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Retrieves a custom attribute value by <paramref name="key"/> or returns <paramref name="defaultValue"/>
        /// when the attribute is not present.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="context">The <see cref="UserContext"/> instance.</param>
        /// <param name="key">The attribute key to look up.</param>
        /// <param name="defaultValue">The value to return when the attribute is missing.</param>
        /// <returns>The attribute value if it exists; otherwise <paramref name="defaultValue"/>.</returns>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException"><paramref name="context"/> is <c>null</c>.</exception>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentException"><paramref name="key"/> is <c>null</c> or empty.</exception>
        public static string? GetCustomAttributeOrDefault(this UserContext context, string key, string? defaultValue = null)
        {
            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(context);
            ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrEmpty(key);

            return context.GetAttribute(key) ?? defaultValue;
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Returns a read‑only dictionary that contains the core user properties together with all custom attributes.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="context">The <see cref="UserContext"/> instance.</param>
        /// <returns>An <see cref="IReadOnlyDictionary{TKey,TValue}"/> of attribute names and values.</returns>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException"><paramref name="context"/> is <c>null</c>.</exception>
        public static IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> GetAllAttributes(this UserContext context)
        {
            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(context);

            var result = new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)
            {
                ["UserId"] = context.UserId,
                ["Email"] = context.Email
            };

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(context.Country))
                result["Country"] = context.Country;

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(context.Tier))
                result["Tier"] = context.Tier;

            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(context.Region))
                result["Region"] = context.Region;

            foreach (var kvp in context.CustomAttributes)
                result[kvp.Key] = kvp.Value;

            return new ReadOnlyDictionary<string, string>(result);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Determines whether the user belongs to the specified <paramref name="tier"/>, using a case‑insensitive comparison.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="context">The <see cref="UserContext"/> instance.</param>
        /// <param name="tier">The tier name to compare against.</param>
        /// <returns><c>true</c> if the user's tier matches <paramref name="tier"/>; otherwise <c>false</c>.</returns>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException"><paramref name="context"/> is <c>null</c>.</exception>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentException"><paramref name="tier"/> is <c>null</c> or empty.</exception>
        public static bool IsInTier(this UserContext context, string tier)
        {
            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(context);
            ArgumentException.ThrowIfNullOrEmpty(tier);

            return string.Equals(context.Tier, tier, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Calculates the age of the user context in whole days based on <see cref="UserContext.CreatedAt"/>.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="context">The <see cref="UserContext"/> instance.</param>
        /// <returns>The number of days elapsed since <see cref="UserContext.CreatedAt"/>.</returns>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException"><paramref name="context"/> is <c>null</c>.</exception>
        public static int GetAgeInDays(this UserContext context)
        {
            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(context);

            // Use UTC to avoid issues with local time zones.
            return (int)(DateTime.UtcNow - context.CreatedAt.ToUniversalTime()).TotalDays;
        }
    }
}
```

src/FeatureFlags/Models/ResultExtensions.cs
```csharp
namespace FeatureFlags.Models;

/// <summary>
/// Provides extension methods for the <see cref="Result"/> and <see cref="Result{T}"/> types.
/// </summary>
public static class ResultExtensions
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Maps the success value of a <see cref="Result{T}"/> to a new value using the provided selector.
    /// If the result is a failure, the failure is propagated.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of the success value.</typeparam>
    /// <typeparam name="TOut">The type of the mapped value.</typeparam>
    /// <param name="result">The result to map.</param>
    /// <param name="selector">The selector to apply to the success value.</param>
    /// <returns>A new <see cref="Result{TOut}"/> that represents the mapped result.</returns>
    /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException">Thrown if <paramref name="selector"/> is null.</exception>
    public static Result<TOut> Map<T, TOut>(this Result<T> result, Func<T, TOut> selector)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(selector);

        return result.IsSuccess
            ? Result<TOut>.Success(selector(result.Data!))
            : Result<TOut>.Failure(result.Error, result.ErrorCode);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Executes the provided action if the <see cref="Result{T}"/> is a success.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of the success value.</typeparam>
    /// <param name="result">The result to evaluate.</param>
    /// <param name="action">The action to execute if the result is a success.</param>
    /// <returns>The original <see cref="Result{T}"/>.</returns>
    /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException">Thrown if <paramref name="action"/> is null.</exception>
    public static Result<T> OnSuccess<T>(this Result<T> result, Action<T> action)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(action);

        if (result.IsSuccess)
        {
            action(result.Data!);
        }

        return result;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Executes the provided action if the <see cref="Result"/> or <see cref="Result{T}"/> is a failure.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of the success value, if any.</typeparam>
    /// <param name="result">The result to evaluate.</param>
    /// <param name="action">The action to execute if the result is a failure.</param>
    /// <returns>The original <see cref="Result{T}"/> or <see cref="Result"/>.</returns>
    /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException">Thrown if <paramref name="action"/> is null.</exception>
    public static Result<T> OnFailure<T>(this Result<T> result, Action<string?, int?> action)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(action);

        if (!result.IsSuccess)
        {
            action(result.Error, result.ErrorCode);
        }

        return result;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// Executes the provided action if the <see cref="Result"/> is a failure.
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="result">The result to evaluate.</param>
    /// <param name="action">The action to execute if the result is a failure.</param>
    /// <returns>The original <see cref="Result"/>.</returns>
    /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException">Thrown if <paramref name="action"/> is null.</exception>
    public static Result OnFailure(this Result result, Action<string?, int?> action)
    {
        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(action);

        if (!result.IsSuccess)
        {
            action(result.Error, result.ErrorCode);
        }

        return result;
    }
}
```

src/FeatureFlags/Models/ABTestVariantExtensions.cs
```
using System;
using System.Globalization;

namespace FeatureFlags.Models
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Provides extension methods for <see cref="ABTestVariant"/> to enhance its functionality.
    /// </summary>
    public static class ABTestVariantExtensions
    {
        /// <summary>
        /// Calculates the conversion rate as a percentage string formatted with two decimal places.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="variant">The AB test variant to calculate the conversion rate for.</param>
        /// <returns>A string representing the conversion rate as a percentage (e.g., "50.00%").</returns>
        /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException">Thrown if <paramref name="variant"/> is null.</exception>
        public static string GetConversionRatePercentageString(this ABTestVariant variant) =>
            variant switch
            {
                null => throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(variant)),
                _ when variant.UserCount == 0 => "0%",
                _ => $"{(variant.ConversionCount / (double)variant.UserCount * 100):F2}%"
            };

        /// <summary>
        /// Determines whether the variant's statistical confidence meets or exceeds the specified threshold.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="variant">The AB test variant to evaluate.</param>
        /// <param name="confidenceThreshold">The minimum confidence level (0-100) required for significance.</param>
